('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tfxmodel = spawn( "script_model", self.origin );\t// spawn a script model')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tfxmodel setmodel ( "tag_origin" );\t\t\t\t// set it to "tag_origin" which is a model with just a "tag_origin" tag')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tfxmodel linkTo ( self );\t\t\t\t\t\t// link it to the parent enitiy which should move with the train')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t// play fx on tag should move the fx with the model, and when the ent is deleted, the fx will go away with it')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\twhile( 1 )')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t{')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\tplayFXontag( level._effect["train_sun_rays"], fxmodel, "tag_origin" );')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\twait( 0.5 );')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t}')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', "\t// instead of ending the thread with this notify, we'll wait until this notify then delete the model")
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tflag_wait( "calling_intro_barrage" );')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\t')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tfxmodel delete();')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '\tself delete();')
('NEWLINE', '\n')
('COMMENT', '}')
